                                    8296     845.     *                                                                  *
                                    8297     846.     *        Main Program Loop                                         *
                                    8298     847.     *                                                                  *
                                    8299     848.     ********************************************************************
                                    8300     849.     *                                                                  *
                                    8301     850.     *  As we read file entries from the Catalog, we check the validity *
                                    8302     851.     *  of the catalog block and the IXR's, and then turn off the       *

0                                  10941    1312.     ********************************************************************
                                   10942    1313.     *                                                                  *
                                   10943    1314.     *  CHECKBIT ROUTINE                                                *
                                   10944    1315.     *                                                                  *
                                   10945    1316.     *   This routine is called to process the bit map.  On the first   *
                                   10946    1317.     *   pass it turns off the appropriate bit in the bit table.  If the*
                                   10947    1318.     *   bit is already off we have an error of class 6.  On the second *
                                   10948    1319.     *   pass, we determine if bit was just off or claimed by someone   *
                                   10949    1320.     *   else (class 7 err).  The second pass only occurs if we have an *
                                   10950    1321.     *   error on the first pass.  During the second pass we must search*
                                   10951    1322.     *   the error list for doubly claimed blocks.  Check it out below. *
                                   10952    1323.     *                                                                  *
                                   10953    1324.     *                                                                  *
                                   10954    1325.     *    |  THE FOLLOWING ERRORS PROCESSED BELOW:                      *
                                   10955    1326.     *    |  TYPE 6: FD BIT NOT ON FOR THIS BLOCK                 PASS 1*
                                   10956    1327.     *    |  TYPE 7: MULTIPLE FILES HAVE  CLAIMED THIS BLKNO      PASS 2*
                                   10957    1328.     *    |           BIT TABLE   0   0   0   0   1   1   1   1         *
                                   10958    1329.     *    |           USER A      0   0   1   1   0   0   1   1         *
                                   10959    1330.     *    |           USER X      0   1   0   1   0   1   0   1         *
                                   10960    1331.     *    |           ERR TYPE   OK   6   6  6/7  LB  OK  OK  7         *
                                   10961    1332.     *                                                                  *
                                   10962    1333.     *                                                                  *
                                   10963    1334.     ********************************************************************
